    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

  <span id="freeText6780290044143547396" style="display:none"><i>This is a previously-published edition - ASIN: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/34753911-neanderthal-seeks-human" rel="nofollow noopener">B00BUWA58E</a></i><br /><br />There are three things you need to know about Janie Morris: 1) She is incapable of engaging in a conversation without volunteering TMTI (Too Much Trivial Information), especially when she is unnerved, 2) No one unnerves her more than Quinn Sullivan, and 3) She doesn't know how to knit.<br /><br />After losing her boyfriend, apartment, and job in the same day, Janie Morris can't help wondering what new torment fate has in store. To her utter mortification, Quinn Sullivan- aka Sir McHotpants- witnesses it all then keeps turning up like a pair of shoes you lust after but can't afford. The last thing she expects is for Quinn- the focus of her slightly, albeit harmless, stalkerish tendencies- to make her an offer she can't refuse.</span>

<a href="/questions/321814-i-am-working-on-a-story-that-takes-place">I am working on a story that takes place in a yarn store. Do you find that your readers like how specific you got with yarn brands? I liked it,but I&#39;m a knitter.</a>

<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/18630626-penny-reid"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1548810992i/18630626._UX100_CR0,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>

<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/18630626-penny-reid">Penny Reid</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">I can always tell when I receive an email from a knitter because they reference the Madelinetosh scene :-)<br/>I was/am careful to include no more than a f<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">I can always tell when I receive an email from a knitter because they reference the Madelinetosh scene :-)<br />I was/am careful to include no more than a few knitting specific details in each of the books as I don't want the actual knitting to overshadow the friendships. Therefore, I make sure the details I do include are efficient "inside jokes" for all my knitting readers.<br /><br />I hope this helps!<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9005639-amy-harmon?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer999994095" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14594910327795673961">I don't review books I don't like. I'm an author and I think there should be some professional courtesy among authors. If you don't like a book and you write books, especially in the Indie community, it is always better to just politely say nothing at all. I know when other authors rate my books poorly and write a critical review it always ticks me off and, frankly, feels a little suspect. Sorry. Just my opinion. SO! Having said that, please believe me when I say, this book rocked and I have no </span>
  <span id="freeText14594910327795673961" style="display:none">I don't review books I don't like. I'm an author and I think there should be some professional courtesy among authors. If you don't like a book and you write books, especially in the Indie community, it is always better to just politely say nothing at all. I know when other authors rate my books poorly and write a critical review it always ticks me off and, frankly, feels a little suspect. Sorry. Just my opinion. SO! Having said that, please believe me when I say, this book rocked and I have no ulterior motive or reason to review it other than I really, really enjoyed it.<br /><br />For me, it was everything I enjoy in a book. <br /><br />I read some reviews of this one before posting my own and I was stunned at some of of the criticisms. First criticism? "It was awkward."<br /> <br />Um. Yeah. It was. It was supposed to be! The heroine is incredibly awkward and cheesy and dorky and she KNITS for hell-sake. And she says the most unbelievably brilliant, yet unimportant, things. And they are FUNNY! Which brings me to another criticism of the book. <br /><br />"There was a lot of irrelevant information." <br /><br />HA HA HA! I'm dying here. YES! There was! The character is a female Alex Trebek without the gravitas and the poise (and the grey hair, etc.)And she was so freaking lovable and endearing. And the stuff this author knows! I was blown away by the attention to factoids and details that for me raise books from "I could read this in a coma and still grasp it" to "Holy crap this is awesome." I like the meat in a book, the stuff that makes the characters real and the story original. And this book has that in spades. And Quinn was sexy. He just was, people. My heart got a little squishy when I typed that. Okay. Back to my point. <br /><br />And finally, this. "I was lost and confused for most of the book. I skimmed most of it."<br /><br />Seriously, if you're going to skim a book, don't complain about not understanding what's going on. o_0 That seems like a given to me. <br /><br />Do I seem a little cranky? Well, I kind of am. I know every book isn't for everyone, but this book was incredibly well-written, intelligent, funny, and just GOOD. And I like good books to get good reviews. <br /><br />That's all. So I'm adding mine to the mix. Plus - I've gifted this book to a handful of my personal friends, one who has a son dying of cancer. She needed a good laugh. And she got one. She contacted me yesterday, thanked me profusely, and said she was "rolling with laughter." <br /><br />Enough said. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14594910327795673961" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/883947167" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/883947167?book_show_action=true">Mar 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer883947167" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4680291681546236790"><b>5 ‘by the mighty power of Thor’ stars!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/43dde3d6-0f73-4001-9fff-9a8129d418ac_zps82f0b8e8.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421143862i/13328580.jpg' alt=' photo 43dde3d6-0f73-4001-9fff-9a8129d418ac_zps82f0b8e8.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><i>Neanderthal Seeks Human</i> really is a smart romance. Smart, funny, sexy and all around wonderful! I listened to this on audio and towards the end found myself doing extra housework and keeping busy just so I could finish it! It was one of those addictive reads I didn’t want to put down! <br/><br/>Janie Morris is one of those heroines you want to be BFF’s with. She’s quirky, intelligent, hilarious and just so fantastically random. Janie has been having a rough time</span>
  <span id="freeText4680291681546236790" style="display:none"><b>5 ‘by the mighty power of Thor’ stars!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/43dde3d6-0f73-4001-9fff-9a8129d418ac_zps82f0b8e8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421143862i/13328580.jpg" alt=" photo 43dde3d6-0f73-4001-9fff-9a8129d418ac_zps82f0b8e8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Neanderthal Seeks Human</i> really is a smart romance. Smart, funny, sexy and all around wonderful! I listened to this on audio and towards the end found myself doing extra housework and keeping busy just so I could finish it! It was one of those addictive reads I didn’t want to put down! <br><br>Janie Morris is one of those heroines you want to be BFF’s with. She’s quirky, intelligent, hilarious and just so fantastically random. Janie has been having a rough time. All within a day she’s broken it off with her boyfriend, lost her apartment, and got downsized from her job. The only upside of all this is that Quinn ‘Sir McHotpants’ Sullivan, security guard, gets to watch it all. Quinn is that guy Janie ogles at work. He’s sexy, strong and he just gets to her. <br><br>After Janie gets laid off, she goes out with a friend only to run into him again. Quinn. They fall into this friendship of sorts. Janie is still awkward as all get out, but Quinn finds it endearing. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/3cfe021f-f983-4158-bbaa-40d8e5618737_zps349bb027.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421143862i/13328581.jpg" alt=" photo 3cfe021f-f983-4158-bbaa-40d8e5618737_zps349bb027.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Janie isn’t one of those girls whose heart flutters when she sees a guy. Never has been. But with Quinn, things are different. She feels different around him. When Janie starts working at a new job, with guess who- Quinn, things get a little tricky. <br><br>Quinn is a wonderful character. I loved how he appreciated Janie for who she was. There was a twist or two with him that readers will catch on to quick, but Janie overlooks. She is so taken by this man. He does things to her, makes her feel things she's never felt before. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/e68a1914-62ed-4d87-a43e-3ec38ce1ebf1_zps34f4267e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421143862i/13328582.jpg" alt=" photo e68a1914-62ed-4d87-a43e-3ec38ce1ebf1_zps34f4267e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I loved watching Janie and Quinn’s relationship grow. I loved all the humor, the laugh out loud moments. I especially loved how relatable Janie was. I also feel a little smarter after reading. Like I have all these random facts in my head now. <br><br>If you’re looking for a fun and feel good read that will make you laugh and smile nonstop with a fantastic heroine and a sexy alpha hero, this is the book for you. The writing was smart, the characters endearing, and it was just so entertaining! I can’t wait to continue on with this series, and I’m especially glad there is another Janie and Quinn book! I’m not ready to let go of these two! <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“God, Quinn, you have no idea how permanent I’d like this to be. I’d like us to be Twinkies and cockroaches, death and taxes.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%206/811ef4aa-3cb0-41fa-b6e7-bd0f3d53e34e_zps29d98375.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer609561257" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14065935369875007192">The thing I HATE about romance books on Goodreads is they always receive this insanely high star rating that is not at all accurate (50 Shades)! It makes me soooo mad! <br/><br/><a href='http://s1299.photobucket.com/user/reblparn/media/annoyed/Creedyoushutup_zpscc0bdf31.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><br/>No, wait, let me calm down and go over the things I liked:<br/>1. It wasn't too bad insta-love which was unusual for how cheesy this whole novel actually was.<br/>2. The protagonist could have been interesting. In a way she was very unique and different.<br/>3. Okay...well I guess that was all I got.<br/><br/>Things I hated:<br/>1. The writing was awful. G</span>
  <span id="freeText14065935369875007192" style="display:none">The thing I HATE about romance books on Goodreads is they always receive this insanely high star rating that is not at all accurate (50 Shades)! It makes me soooo mad! <br><br><a href="http://s1299.photobucket.com/user/reblparn/media/annoyed/Creedyoushutup_zpscc0bdf31.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420719ra/834914.gif" alt=" photo Creedyoushutup_zpscc0bdf31.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>No, wait, let me calm down and go over the things I liked:<br>1. It wasn't too bad insta-love which was unusual for how cheesy this whole novel actually was.<br>2. The protagonist could have been interesting. In a way she was very unique and different.<br>3. Okay...well I guess that was all I got.<br><br>Things I hated:<br>1. The writing was awful. Grammatical errors, spelling errors, weird phrasing, strange metaphors... it was all bad.<br>2. The plot was ludicrous. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Janie literally ended up with a man just like her ex-boyfriend. The reasons they broke up were exactly WHY she liked the new fellow. Am I missing something here? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>3.The conversations were often so awkward I cringed. Is it always necessary to make your two leads so dumb that they always misunderstand what the other means, and follow that up with some unnecessary angst!<br>4.Dude was too controlling! Cannot. stand. that. It is not romantic, believe me.<br>5. Was this written in present tense or past because I'm not sure the author knew?<br><br>I started highlighting stuff that made me laugh out loud about halfway through. I will include it below for anyone who wants a good giggle:<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <i> I didn’t understand men. They made no sense and behave erratically.<br><br>Marie shook her head, “Four weeks is long enough. People have fallen head over heels in less time than that.”</i><br><br> <b>Really? Do most people fall completely in love with strangers? <br><br><a href="http://s1299.photobucket.com/user/reblparn/media/annoyed/tumblr_lx9j1syNSr1qdrpdr_zps057f142b.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420719ra/834915.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lx9j1syNSr1qdrpdr_zps057f142b.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br>That is an exception...not the norm.</b> <br><br><i>The combined pressure of performing at the client meeting and proving I deserved to work at Cypher Systems along with the thought of seeing Quinn for the first time in a week, now as ‘the Boss’, caused my stomach to became like the hair trapped in bubblegum- heinous, untenable knots.</i><br><br><a href="http://s1299.photobucket.com/user/reblparn/media/disgusted/tumblr_mdps58rYc41qzwfvn_zps6664dec0.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420719ra/834916.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mdps58rYc41qzwfvn_zps6664dec0.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br> <b>GROSS.</b><br><br><i>Abruptly, he wrapped the long fingers of one hand around my neck and, before I could think or react, he dragged his mouth over mine then ransacked.<br><br>His tenderness- of his voice, touch- filled me with the acute need to invade the silence.</i> <b>Such an awkward sentence.</b><br><br><i>My half laugh was involuntary, immediate, as were my words, “God, Quinn, you have no idea how permanent I’d like this to be. I’d like us to be twinkies and cockroaches, death and taxes. But I-”</i> <br><br><a href="http://s1299.photobucket.com/user/reblparn/media/tumblr_mak1dsMJ351qzdjv6_zps77174f95.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420719ra/834917.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mak1dsMJ351qzdjv6_zps77174f95.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><b>WTF?</b><br><br><i>“Seriously, big guy, you just need to make like a shepherd and get the flock out of here.” Sandra crossed her arms over her chest, her voice low with warning.</i><br><br><a href="http://s1299.photobucket.com/user/reblparn/media/tumblr_inline_mq0w149scC1qz4rgp_zps5e30c9ad.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420719ra/834918.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_mq0w149scC1qz4rgp_zps5e30c9ad.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><b>Such an enormous amount of cheesiness. I don't think there was a single character I wouldn't have wanted to hit in the face five minutes after meeting them.</b><br><br><br><i>I swear, the next time Janie’s hot boyfriend saves ya’all from neck tattooed goons, ya’all better wait till I’m done with my shift or else I’m gunna be pissed.”</i> <b>Just sloppy.</b><br><br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1257182707" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1257182707" />
    <a title="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31461418-alienor-french-frowner"><img alt="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1532688964p2/31461418.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1257182707?book_show_action=true">Apr 17, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" href="/user/show/31461418-alienor-french-frowner">Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘ by: </span>
      GR
  </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1257182707" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1860394072723288982"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429295103i/14566469._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>DNF 64%</b> : <b>This kind of book reminds me why I barely read chick-lit anymore</b>. I mean, I could probably finish it, but then my Kindle would be in a great deal of peril I guess. I can't do this. <br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436496217ra/15468305.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Exceptionally my list review won't be positive, as in, it's more everything that I DON'T want to find in my romance than anything else. <br/><br/>I certainly don't want a so-called special snow-flake as an heroine with whom I enter in OH COME ON territory right away.<br/><br/>► <b>She thinks she's not attractive, while she obviou</b></span>
  <span id="freeText1860394072723288982" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429295103i/14566469._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>DNF 64%</b> : <b>This kind of book reminds me why I barely read chick-lit anymore</b>. I mean, I could probably finish it, but then my Kindle would be in a great deal of peril I guess. I can't do this. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436496217ra/15468305.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Exceptionally my list review won't be positive, as in, it's more everything that I DON'T want to find in my romance than anything else. <br><br>I certainly don't want a so-called special snow-flake as an heroine with whom I enter in OH COME ON territory right away.<br><br>► <b>She thinks she's not attractive, while she obviously IS</b> : <i>"You're beautiful, even if you don't believe it. A lot of guys, and, I mean, a lot of guys, like the big boobs, small waist, big butt, long legs, amazon woman thing you have going on."</i> <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436496217ra/15468306.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>She RAMBLES - think verbal diarrhea</b> and maybe Quinn thinks it's cute, I mean, GOOD FOR YOU MAN, but personally I found it obnoxious and I just wanted for her to shut the hell up. So, yes, she knows a lot of random facts and it's supposed to mean that she's clever and all, and I guess that it's meant for me, <i>normal girl</i>, to relate or something but really? <b>She is exhausting, and border condescending at times</b>. <br><br><i>"Did the real world actually exist if everyone only interacted via cell phones? Would Angry Birds one day become my reality? Was I the unsuspecting pig or the exploding bird? These Descartes-based musings rarely made me popular at parties."</i><br><br>OH COME ON. Cut the shit, would you? They're by no means "Descartes-based musings". You want Descartes?<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436496217i/15468307._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Muse on this, Jani. <br><br>Perhaps I'm not enough clear of why I think she's not that clever : it's because for me we need to look beyond the academic or non-academic knowledge - someone literate isn't necessarily clever, and the contrary is also true. I graduated in Literature in College and knew a great deal of people who thought they were clever because they were full of quotes, and thought it was okay to belittle my coworkers at McDonald's because some of them didn't go to college. I HATE THAT SHIT. First it's incredibly pedant and secondly it's just not <i>true</i>.<br><br>Now, excuse me, but <b>someone who doesn't realize that she's dating her fucking BOSS during WEEKS makes me lose patience</b>. I mean FOR REAL. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436496217i/15468308._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Not to mention a passage where she and her friend are offered drinks by a stranger in a bar (by stranger I mean that they don't even SEE him), and decide to drink them <i>"dutifully"</i>after the barman tells them that he would be in trouble if they didn't. FOR FUCK SAKE. I mean GHB, anyone?<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436496217i/15468309.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>She puts labels on people (and she glorifies it), and more than that, she slut-shames</b>. This passage particularly infuriated me : <br><br><i>"See the plastic-looking ones on the purple lily pad? I would call a group like that a latex of ladies, with the word latex being the collective noun. And those cages, with the monkeys and the couples - I would call them collectively a vulgar of cages, with the word vulgar being the collective noun."<br>He lifted his hand to get the bartender's attention as he spoke. "I would switch them. I would call the cages a latex of cages and the women a vulgar of women."</i><br><br>ISN'T IT BLOODY WONDERFUL?<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436496217i/15468310.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► She is finding <i>excuses</i> for her ex-boyfriend who cheated on her, and expresses how she should have see it coming because HEY GUYS! He was <b>too good to be true</b>. Like a guy can't be attractive, wealthy, interesting and trust-worthy. <b>I find this kind of comments unbelievably insulting for all the faithful guys out there</b>.<br><br>► Her ex-boyfriend was incredibly controlling, and she was (understandably) tired of it so what does she do? <b>She finds another control prick</b>. I'm sorry, Quinn isn't a bad guy and is yummy, I guess, but <b>he IS controlling</b> on many occasions. Example?<br><br><i>"I picked up the menu to make a hurried selection, but for the second time in our short acquaintance, Quinn did that thing you see in movies but don't ever experience in real life : Without asking for my opinion, he ordered for me."</i><br><br>Is that just me? I would HATE this. <b>This is not romantic. Someone who cares about you cares about WHAT YOU WANT</b>. That and the fact that sorry, but glares don't appeal to me one bit. Therefore I'm not saying Quinn is a HUGE asshole, but as I couldn't stand rambling judgmental Janie I would have needed an adorable and swoon-worthy male-lead to make me want to finish. <b>He wasn't.</b><br><br>PS : I guess it's not my kind of humor because I never ever laughed. Except if you count the "OMG what did I just read I can't believe it" kind of laughs.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397096722ra/9230537.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i><br><blockquote>
  <a href="https://meetthebookworld.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487851828i/22057164._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1218658611" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2067025549540094768"><strong>Heartwarming And Hilarious</strong><br/><br/>I thoroughly enjoyed this story. 'Neanderthal Seeks Human' was a sweet, laugh-out-loud, romance. I was smiling like a loon while I listened to this story during my daily commute. I'm sure the other drivers thought I was off my rocker.<br/><br/> Right from the start, I felt like I had been pulled into Janie's orbit. She isn't your typical heroine. In fact, she's kind of weird...but in a totally endearing way. Always rambling on about some little known, and often irrelevant, fact, </span>
  <span id="freeText2067025549540094768" style="display:none"><strong>Heartwarming And Hilarious</strong><br /><br />I thoroughly enjoyed this story. 'Neanderthal Seeks Human' was a sweet, laugh-out-loud, romance. I was smiling like a loon while I listened to this story during my daily commute. I'm sure the other drivers thought I was off my rocker.<br /><br /> Right from the start, I felt like I had been pulled into Janie's orbit. She isn't your typical heroine. In fact, she's kind of weird...but in a totally endearing way. Always rambling on about some little known, and often irrelevant, fact, she definitely had her share of quirks. <br /><br />When Janie catches her boyfriend cheating on her, she promptly dumps him and heads to work. Only, she finds out that she's being mysteriously fired. So, the story starts with her "worst day ever". I immediately identified with Janie and her horrible luck. Who hasn't had a day like that?<br /><br />To top it off, she's escorted out of the building by the ultra-sexy security guard that she'd spent the last several months secretly crushing on, Quinn. Despite having an audience for her mortification, she managed to draw his interest...and sympathy. He hooks her up with a job at his company and helps her get back on her feet.<br /><br />Of course, things are not exactly what they appear to be. As Janie and Quinn's relationship starts to get serious, some truths come to light that threaten to ruin everything. Meanwhile, Janie's crazy sister is wreaking havoc and her cheating ex-boyfriend is determined to work his way back into her life. There is plenty of drama to keep this story entertaining.<br /><br />Overall, I thought this was a fun, lighthearted read/listen. The Audible narration was well-done. The characters were endearing and easy to relate to. Quinn was a hot, quiet, Alpha. What's not to love? Sure, it was a bit predictable, but I didn't care. This story was a good time and a great way to pass some time.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2067025549540094768" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer638022163" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17799911572932317846"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472750173i/20237706._SX540_.jpg' width='200' height='150' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>*2.5 stars* <br/><br/>I'm not trying to be Debbie Downer over here, but with all the hype with this story, I was just expecting... more. <br/><br/>This book is described as a "smart romance," when in reality it is simply the typical trope of the billionaire/millionaire player guy with baggage who doesn't want to settle down for anyone but makes an exception for his special snowflake, who happens to be a naive, virgin-esk young girl. (aka, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10818853.Fifty_Shades_of_Grey__Fifty_Shades___1_' title='Fifty Shades of Grey (Fifty Shades, #1) by E.L. James' rel='nofollow noopener'>Fifty Shades of Grey</a>) And Jane is too tall (!) with too big of a butt and boo</span>
  <span id="freeText17799911572932317846" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472750173i/20237706._SX540_.jpg" width="200" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*2.5 stars* <br><br>I'm not trying to be Debbie Downer over here, but with all the hype with this story, I was just expecting... more. <br><br>This book is described as a "smart romance," when in reality it is simply the typical trope of the billionaire/millionaire player guy with baggage who doesn't want to settle down for anyone but makes an exception for his special snowflake, who happens to be a naive, virgin-esk young girl. (aka, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10818853.Fifty_Shades_of_Grey__Fifty_Shades___1_" title="Fifty Shades of Grey (Fifty Shades, #1) by E.L. James" rel="nofollow noopener">Fifty Shades of Grey</a>) And Jane is too tall (!) with too big of a butt and boobs that are too big (!), but doesn't realize she is attractive at all... of course. <br><br>I'm not saying that this book is bad, because it isn't, but it isn't anything out of the ordinary, even including putting a geeky, socially EXTREMELY unaware girl as the MC. I couldn't understand how she didn't pick up on her security guard <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[actually being the big boss <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. No one could be that dense, especially after the 100s of clues. <br><br>My main issue is that this story dragged on and on. I listened as an audiobook, which was nicely narrated, and I felt like nothing happened! It is a loooong audiobook, over 14 hours, and I literally couldn't take it anymore at about 10 hours. It was too much, too much of a TSTL female MC and the bossy male MC that I've seen before. It felt like it needed to be edited down by 100 pages (or 4 hours) to be cohesive and well-paced, and it felt VERY self-pubbed to me. <br><br>I guess I'm just not seeing what everyone else did. Sure, I enjoyed when Jane spouted some obscure facts and was entertained by her oddities, but that can only take a book so far. </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_3561913911" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3561913911" />
    <a title="chan ☆" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/48727754-chan"><img alt="chan ☆" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1596680961p2/48727754.jpg" /></a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3561913911?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="chan ☆" class="user" itemprop="url" name="chan ☆" href="/user/show/48727754-chan">chan ☆</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/52422311-neanderthal-seeks-human">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48727754-chan?shelf=2020">2020</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48727754-chan?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3561913911" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9605450525422849997"><b>an impressive debut, but not an impressive novel otherwise</b><br/><br/>if you're looking for a book that has the same effect as say, binge watching episodes of new girl, i think you're in the right place. if you're looking for a life changing, swoon worthy romance... i'd look elsewhere.<br/><br/>this was a perfectly acceptable office romance with a quirky heroine and stoic hero. which now that i think of it... is the set up for most office romances. and i think that was my main issue with the book. it was well written</span>
  <span id="freeText9605450525422849997" style="display:none"><b>an impressive debut, but not an impressive novel otherwise</b><br /><br />if you're looking for a book that has the same effect as say, binge watching episodes of new girl, i think you're in the right place. if you're looking for a life changing, swoon worthy romance... i'd look elsewhere.<br /><br />this was a perfectly acceptable office romance with a quirky heroine and stoic hero. which now that i think of it... is the set up for most office romances. and i think that was my main issue with the book. it was well written, if a bit verbose (like seriously should have been cut down by 150 pages verbose), but it was just... unoriginal. not bad, just boring.<br /><br />and life is too short for boring. unless you need something to soothe you to sleep via audio, which i might actually recommend.</span>

<div id="review_741876857" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/741876857" />
    <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole"><img alt="Duchess Nicole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499265843p2/2204947.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/741876857?book_show_action=true">Oct 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Duchess Nicole" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole">Duchess Nicole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Duchess Nicole by: </span>
       ★Jennifer★ aka PHER 
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=humorous">humorous</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=e-pcs">e-pcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-contemp-romance">genre-contemp-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=4-star-read">4-star-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=self-contained">self-contained</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer741876857" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7362192716957556675"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383060099i/6366063._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/>This was SUCH a fun read. Funny, funny, funny, with a side of nerdy humor and a few little twists that keep the story interesting, it was hard to put down. <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383058772i/6365094._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Janie is one of the quirkiest and most unforgettable characters. She's super smart but not socially savvy. She loves designer heels and has a constant run of trivial facts running through her overactive brain that she ends up spouting when she's nervous. The book starts out on the worst day in her recent memory, the day she catches her longt</span>
  <span id="freeText7362192716957556675" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383060099i/6366063._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>This was SUCH a fun read. Funny, funny, funny, with a side of nerdy humor and a few little twists that keep the story interesting, it was hard to put down. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383058772i/6365094._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Janie is one of the quirkiest and most unforgettable characters. She's super smart but not socially savvy. She loves designer heels and has a constant run of trivial facts running through her overactive brain that she ends up spouting when she's nervous. The book starts out on the worst day in her recent memory, the day she catches her longtime live in boyfriend cheating, realizes that she's actually not very upset about it, which is upsetting, she loses her job, and to top it all off, she's out of toilet paper. After an embarrassing escort out of her office building by the super sexy "Sir McHotpants" (Quinn) security guard and random limo ride home, it's official. <br><br><b>Worst. <br>Day. <br>Ever.</b><br><br>But it seems that one good thing DID come from that awful day...she caught the attention of Sir McHotpants, and he seems determined to either take care of her, or buddy up to her, or be something...more.<br><b>
  <blockquote>"It felt like we were becoming friends or, at least, friendly. I didn't see him as just a delicious piece of man meat any more. I saw him as Quinn; pushy, intelligent, frustrating, sexy Quinn who liked to tease me and thought I was smart and talented."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Quinn is quite the enigma, and while the twist that follows him around just waiting to jump out at you is fairly obvious to the reader, Janie remains oblivious. Oblivious and smitten, but so gun-shy and down on herself and her rambling mouth that she lets her insecurities get in the way of a relationship. Especially because Quinn is just so utterly delicious.<br><b>
  <blockquote>"If we were in Victorian England I would have called him dashing; but, since we lived in the 21st Century I would have to settle for the wordier <i>GQ model hot.</i>."</blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383060099i/6366064.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Janie has quite the group of crazy friends. They like to get together in their knitting group...although Janie doesn't knit, and really, this is the only time knitting is involved in any way shape or form. I was somewhat put off by the knitting in the title, because...uh, who knits any more? And who wants to read about it? Don't worry, it has nothing to do with the story. This group of women is just a bunch of zany friends. They gossip, they talk men and fashion and fun.<br><b>
  <blockquote>"You all remember McHotpants, the security guard? Well, Janie and I saw him at that new club where the naked ladies dance with the monkeys, his name is Quinn, and she went home with him after being drugged. they had breakfast together Saturday and he got her the interview for her new job."<br>It was like throwing Hustler magazines at sex addicts."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>The friends see Janie as most friends do: a wonderful, beautiful woman deserving of someone equally special. And this is Janie and Quinn's journey...it's crazy and nerdy, full of inane facts that you will likely never use in real life, but seriously...this was so much fun. I'd compare it to Alice Clayton or Belle Aurora but without the sexy times. My biggeest complaint is the lack of steam. I can do without a ton of description, but I can't do without sex. And for me, it was such a glaring miss...I felt the loss, as if there was just a gap in the story. The language outside of the bedroom and the light sexual focus of the characters led me to believe that there would be more, and sadly, there wasn't. So that's where the lack of five stars comes from.<br><br>I most definitely recommend this to anyone who's in the mood for lighthearted and fun romance, a self contained love story with room for series growth.<br><br>A huge thanks to my friendly Other for the rec!<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="7362192716957556675" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1360727866" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2015551100252154871"><b>3 long winded stars</b><br/><br/><a href='https://imgur.com/uZ7hqkp' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1529539844ra/25827927.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b> Mild Spoilers ahead</b><br/><br/>I really thought I would like Neanderthal Seeks Human more than I did. All my friends loved it and here I am again the minority, because I really didn't get into this read. I read some reviews that said this book was so funny, but I didn't laugh, not once. I kept wondering if I was reading the same books as everyone else. It's not that I hated the book, because I didn't. I sat after reading this book for 12 hours to try to figure out why I just didn't c</span>
  <span id="freeText2015551100252154871" style="display:none"><b>3 long winded stars</b><br><br><a href="https://imgur.com/uZ7hqkp" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1529539844ra/25827927.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> Mild Spoilers ahead</b><br><br>I really thought I would like Neanderthal Seeks Human more than I did. All my friends loved it and here I am again the minority, because I really didn't get into this read. I read some reviews that said this book was so funny, but I didn't laugh, not once. I kept wondering if I was reading the same books as everyone else. It's not that I hated the book, because I didn't. I sat after reading this book for 12 hours to try to figure out why I just didn't connect to this book and I only thing I can think of is it's too long winded. See when I started the book I really liked Janie. I thought she was cute, quirky, and different. About halfway through the book though her constant purple prose interior monologue started to get annoying. Then I got bored. On top of that I never got a good feel for Quinn as he was hard to read. We never got his pov, and had to learn about him through Janie who was socially awkward. I never got to see any real depth to Quinn. Still it wasn't a bad read and I think if the book was shorter or it had dual pov, maybe a few less Janie mind rants and I would have enjoyed it much more. </span>
  <a data-text-id="2015551100252154871" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Flo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7643503-flo"><img alt="Flo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597575025p2/7643503.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1231895244?book_show_action=true">Mar 19, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Flo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Flo" href="/user/show/7643503-flo">Flo</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=humour">humour</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1231895244" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10359275151952607864"><b>4 **<u>Hotty McHotpants</u>** STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434974638i/15286117.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Men should come with manuals, subtitles, and reset buttons.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>I'm still smiling. So adorable and cute and funny and weird. A really fantastic read or listen if you will. I did a little mix of ebook and audiobook here and it was delightful. The narrator had an amazing voice and I really enjoyed listening to her. I actually lost quite a few hours over the last two days being sucked into Janie's world and I don't regret one second of it.<br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17673307-neanderthal-seeks-human' rel='nofollow noopener'>Neanderthal Seeks Human</a></span>
  <span id="freeText10359275151952607864" style="display:none"><b>4 **<u>Hotty McHotpants</u>** STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434974638i/15286117.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Men should come with manuals, subtitles, and reset buttons.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I'm still smiling. So adorable and cute and funny and weird. A really fantastic read or listen if you will. I did a little mix of ebook and audiobook here and it was delightful. The narrator had an amazing voice and I really enjoyed listening to her. I actually lost quite a few hours over the last two days being sucked into Janie's world and I don't regret one second of it.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17673307-neanderthal-seeks-human" rel="nofollow noopener">Neanderthal Seeks Human</a> was my very first full <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5997227.Penny_Reid" rel="nofollow noopener">Penny Reid</a> book. I know that's crazy, right? Well, I read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23285659-the-hooker-and-the-hermit" rel="nofollow noopener">The Hooker and the Hermit</a> before, but that was co-authored with Ms. Cosway. In any case I'm really pleasantly surprised how much I enjoyed this book and I can't wait to read the rest in the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/101713-knitting-in-the-city" rel="nofollow noopener">Knitting in the City</a> series. <br><br>Let's talk story...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“She said I owned the clothes of a radiologist and the shoes of an OBGYN; which is like the medical doctor equivalent of saying that I dressed like a librarian with a propensity of fuckmeboots.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Janie Morris</b> has the worst day of her life. She broke up with her boyfriend after he cheated on her. Her heels broke on the way to work. The outfit is ruined by spilled coffee. She just got fired from her job and then on top of that Mr. Hotty McHotpants decides it's the right day to talk to her for the first time. It's all a nightmare, really.<br><br>Janie is the epitome of quirkiness and has an extreme case of foot in mouth syndrome. She is highly intelligent, but equipped with barely any social skills. Anytime she tries to talk to a man it ends up with a verbal diarrhoea, and not just any old kind of rambling. No, Janie is a special girl with a very exceptional brain. She knows things, random things and she likes to share. Especially when she is nervous.<br><br>I have to say, she takes some getting used to. I'm sure there are people who find her annoying and can't stand her unusual kind of crazy, but I fell in love with her very early on. Not going to lie, there were times when I wanted to strangle her, but then she did something so sweet that I just fell hard all over again.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435054651ra/15295619.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“My brain finds you more interesting than all the really interesting trivial facts I could be contemplating or researching at present.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Quinn Sullivan</b>. Mmmmh... What can I tell you about Sir McHotpants? He is very yummy to look at. Obviously. Janie catches his eye as he works in her office building as an afternoon security guard and on that faithful day she gets laid off Mr. McHotpants escorts her out of the building. After that, well let's just say their paths cross again and again. *wink wink*<br><br>Quinn is the silent stoic type. Very little words, but his actions speak volumes. He is kind, considerate and has the patience of a saint, but he is also very much in control, with a dash of dominance on the side. I really, really liked him. <br><br>And the two together? Magical.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I wondered what steps I could take to remove the word ‘moisture’ or even ‘moist’ from the English language; I really hated the way it sounded and always went out of my way to avoid saying it. I also really didn’t like the word slacks.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><i>Neanderthal Seeks Human</i> is one of those books where you should carefully consider your preferences before you pick it up. Are you in the mood for cuteness overflow? Are you willing to hear endless rants, witness ridiculous misunderstandings and sugar sweet chick-flick goodness? Then go right ahead and get on it. If any of those things make your teeth ache stay far away from it. Just FYI. <br><br>It's a feel good read through and through. Light, funny, sweet. What else do you want?<br><br>Oh, I know...did I mention Janie has a posse of knitting girlfriends? Well, they all play a significant role and the ladies get books of their own. Next stop <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18001399-friends-without-benefits" rel="nofollow noopener">Friends Without Benefits</a>, but first the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18875842-neanderthal-marries-human" rel="nofollow noopener">Neanderthal Marries Human</a>. I'm going to be stuck in chick flick heaven for a while. Send help. ;D<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431601625i/14852808.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/coffeeaddictbooks?ref=tn_tnmn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598100i/14852514.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/flo_reads" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852521.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852522.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/101016591301224002138" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852523.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/flocoffeeaddict/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431599699i/14852627.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Belle Aurora" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Belle Aurora" href="/user/show/18164357-belle-aurora">Belle Aurora</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer718364859" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12807630836111398718">When I told Penny that I was reading her book, *chuckles* she flipped out! And I really have NO IDEA why! She was all "This might not be the book for you. She is very awkward and nerdy. Don't feel bad if you don't like it..."<br/><br/>*Insert hysterical laughter here*<br/><br/>Seriously! WHAT A FREAKING GREAT BOOK!!! This was not a 4.5 star read for me...It was a straight out 5!<br/><br/>I'll tell you exactly what I liked about this book.<br/>Firstly, Janie. How on earth can you not fall in love with this lady??!<br/>She reminded me s</span>
  <span id="freeText12807630836111398718" style="display:none">When I told Penny that I was reading her book, *chuckles* she flipped out! And I really have NO IDEA why! She was all "This might not be the book for you. She is very awkward and nerdy. Don't feel bad if you don't like it..."<br /><br />*Insert hysterical laughter here*<br /><br />Seriously! WHAT A FREAKING GREAT BOOK!!! This was not a 4.5 star read for me...It was a straight out 5!<br /><br />I'll tell you exactly what I liked about this book.<br />Firstly, Janie. How on earth can you not fall in love with this lady??!<br />She reminded me somewhat of the woman, main character from the series BONES. She's just FULL of random facts and knowledge, which not only was intriguing but she decided to pull the randomness out at the most awkward times which led to me having to set my kindle down to LAUGH MY ASS OFF!!!<br />Secondly, Quinn. Regardless of how he comes across, he is an alpha. He is protective and loyal, and best of all, SWEET! What a sweetheart! Swoon!<br />Thirdly, the writing. Penny has a way with words. I found myself re-reading sentences just to take them in further because this book is just SPECIAL. It's seriously on my all-time faves list now. <br />You know sometimes authors fill a book with sex and write their story around that. Sometimes its necessary. In this book, it was not. There was very little steam in this book but mountains of sexual tension, which for me, is just as satisfying.<br /><br />In short, Love Love LOVED this book! I will re-read it.<br />Can't wait to get onto the next one!<br /><br />Belle x</span>

<div id="review_878835805" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/878835805" />
    <a title="Catarina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina"><img alt="Catarina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514808293p2/11538033.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/878835805?book_show_action=true">Mar 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Catarina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Catarina" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina">Catarina</a>
      </span>

        rated it

<span id="freeTextContainer5341825496723636327"><b>5 Fluffy and Warm Stars!</b>	<br/><br/>Describe what I felt about this book in one sentence it’s pretty easy: <br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/617638.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Okay. <br/>So, Janie had a pretty bad day. She lost her job, her home and found out her long-time boyfriend is a cheater. So yeah, not a sunny day for her. <br/>Enters Quinn. He got her an interview and she has now a new job, a new house… a new friendship with Quinn. <br/>But somehow along the way that friendship starts to grow into something more and is time to bring back the secrets, fears and ghosts from the pas</span>
  <span id="freeText5341825496723636327" style="display:none"><b>5 Fluffy and Warm Stars!</b>	<br><br>Describe what I felt about this book in one sentence it’s pretty easy: <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/617638.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Okay. <br>So, Janie had a pretty bad day. She lost her job, her home and found out her long-time boyfriend is a cheater. So yeah, not a sunny day for her. <br>Enters Quinn. He got her an interview and she has now a new job, a new house… a new friendship with Quinn. <br>But somehow along the way that friendship starts to grow into something more and is time to bring back the secrets, fears and ghosts from the past: and both of them have a great deal of them. <br>Luckily Janie has her knit group to support her, and believe me, balls of yarn were never funnier! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388683472i/7901653.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 5 Stars. <br> <b>Storyline: </b> Not completely original and unexpected, but don’t let that stop you. This is an amazing reading that will leave with warm feelings in your stomach (in a good way!). Not to mention you will have a good laugh with it. Definitely, a series to follow. <br> <b>Writing Style: </b> First person, female POV. Amazingly written and addictive. You will not put it down. My only complaint? It needed a longer epilogue!<br> <b>Character Development: </b> I loved Janie. Even with all insecurities she is probably one of my favorite heroines ever. She is funny, and sweetly weird and I loved her sense of humor. Not to mention all the random things she says are awesome. Quinn is a perfect alpha-male and I love him. No, seriously, LOVE HIM! That’s all. <br>I loved the supportive characters, I can’t wait to read Elizabeth’s story. <br> <b>Steam: </b> Mild. And that’s the only bad thing about this book. It lacked steam, all the steamy parts were shortened. :(<br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1229311237" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1229311237" />
    <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously"><img alt="Rachel Reads Ravenously" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539149211p2/14514998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1229311237?book_show_action=true">Mar 16, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Reads Ravenously" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously">Rachel Reads Ravenously</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=new-adult-mania">new-adult-mania</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1229311237" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10583211769895595260"><b> 3.75 really cute stars!!! </b><br/><br/><b> <i> “She said I owned the clothes of a radiologist and the shoes of an OBGYN; which is like the medical doctor equivalent of saying that I dressed like a librarian with a propensity of fuckmeboots.” </i> </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/neanderthal%20seeks%20human.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426742580i/14088054._SX540_.png' alt=' photo neanderthal seeks human.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This is my second Penny Reid book and it was a lot of fun! I had originally only read The Hooker and the Hermit, and now it's very clear to me who wrote what in that book now that I've read books by both authors.<br/><br/><b> Neanderthal Seeks Human </b> is about Janie who just broke up </span>
  <span id="freeText10583211769895595260" style="display:none"><b> 3.75 really cute stars!!! </b><br><br><b> <i> “She said I owned the clothes of a radiologist and the shoes of an OBGYN; which is like the medical doctor equivalent of saying that I dressed like a librarian with a propensity of fuckmeboots.” </i> </b><br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/neanderthal%20seeks%20human.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426742580i/14088054._SX540_.png" alt=" photo neanderthal seeks human.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This is my second Penny Reid book and it was a lot of fun! I had originally only read The Hooker and the Hermit, and now it's very clear to me who wrote what in that book now that I've read books by both authors.<br><br><b> Neanderthal Seeks Human </b> is about Janie who just broke up with her boyfriend, spilled coffee on herself, broke her shoes and got fired from her job. She is escorted out of her office building by a security guard also know to her (privately) as McHotPants. Janie is a bit socially awkward, she has a tendency to spew out random facts at the drop of a hat. But Janie is really smart, and a bit aloof as to how pretty she is. A series of chance meetings with McHotPants aka Quinn, lands Janie a new job. And that's all I will say for now...<br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/pagebreak.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421135336i/13327545.png" alt=" photo pagebreak.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I really liked Quinn as a hero. He wasn't the most decisive guy, but he seemed to really like Janie for who she was and was genuinely interested in all of her random factoids. It also took him forever to show Janie he liked her, but to be fair, she was oblivious to many things throughout the book. And I liked that about Janie, because quite honestly, it made her relatable (to me, because I am super oblivious quite a bit of the time as well).<br><br><b> <i> “I decided, as I succumbed to sleep, that men should come with manuals, subtitles, and reset buttons.” </i> </b><br><br>This book had fairly low angst and no over the top drama, which many of you enjoy. The one thing it really needed though was a little bit more steam and a little less fade to black. <br><br>At times I found myself laughing out loud in places I shouldn't have. There is a very funny knitting group meeting near the end that I could not stop laughing at and had to set my kindle down before I dropped it. I also spent a lot of time reading this when I should have been doing grad work, so it's highly addictive too.<br><br>Give it a chance! It's a great read for when you don't know what to read next :)</span>
  <a data-text-id="10583211769895595260" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
