<div id="review_1278932292" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1278932292" />
    <a title="Tamara" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7466356-tamara"><img alt="Tamara" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1392836607p2/7466356.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1278932292?book_show_action=true">May 12, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tamara" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tamara" href="/user/show/7466356-tamara">Tamara</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/21519852-neanderthal-seeks-human">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7466356-tamara?shelf=will-never-re-read-again">will-never-re-read-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7466356-tamara?shelf=cliche">cliche</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7466356-tamara?shelf=somebody-pour-me-a-drink">somebody-pour-me-a-drink</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7466356-tamara?shelf=special-little-snowflake">special-little-snowflake</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7466356-tamara?shelf=heroes-heroines-on-my-shit-list">heroes-heroines-on-my-shit-list</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7466356-tamara?shelf=dont-know-why-i-read-it">dont-know-why-i-read-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7466356-tamara?shelf=meh-characters">meh-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7466356-tamara?shelf=2015-reads">2015-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7466356-tamara?shelf=so-hard-to-read-finish">so-hard-to-read-finish</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7466356-tamara?shelf=books-i-end-up-hating">books-i-end-up-hating</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1278932292" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16406115343878460205">Smart romance my ass.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431559139ra/14848492.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Too fucking cheesy.</b><br/><br/>I've started reading this out of boredom but ended up feeling even more bored. How the hell that happened? The only highlight of my day was seeing Avengers Age of Ultron with my friends but even that cant cure what what this book causing: TOTAL BOREDOOM.<br/><br/>The book starts with insta lust, continues with insta lust and oh there's also a bit of insta-love going on. <b>Even worse; the main character is one of the most cluelesst, naive and annoying heroines I've see</b></span>
  <span id="freeText16406115343878460205" style="display:none">Smart romance my ass.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431559139ra/14848492.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Too fucking cheesy.</b><br><br>I've started reading this out of boredom but ended up feeling even more bored. How the hell that happened? The only highlight of my day was seeing Avengers Age of Ultron with my friends but even that cant cure what what this book causing: TOTAL BOREDOOM.<br><br>The book starts with insta lust, continues with insta lust and oh there's also a bit of insta-love going on. <b>Even worse; the main character is one of the most cluelesst, naive and annoying heroines I've seen.</b><br><br>Every time she thinks something or opens her mouth to talk I wanted to bang my head to the wall. She is a TSTL heroine. She's too fucking clueless ok? Use your brain woman, use your fucking brain!! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431788410ra/14866876.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story starts with the heroine losing her job. The security guard she had a crush on aka McHotpants, assists her out of the building. She never asks why, stupidly tries to justify it. The McHotpants, aka Quinn arranges her a limousine so she can go home but she never asks why, just tries to stupidly justify it. Goes to a club with a friend, gets drunk, Quinn who is also there tells her to not go to the Canopy room and never come to club alone. She never asks why and never even tries to justify it this time. <b>She doesnt listen, goes to the room and gets drugged, wakes up in Quinn's house and believes in whatever the hell he says and she never even asks herself why.</b><br><br>WTF?<br><br>SEE THE PATERN?<br><br><b>THIS GIRL IS FUCKING RETARDED.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431788410ra/14866877.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She is completely blind to the obvious. Here is what a 'normal' people would have thought if they were in her shoes.<br><br><b>1)</b> Why the fuck would a security guard would accompany you when you are leaving the building? (It's not like you did something horrible to lose your job. You did nothing.)<br><br><b>2)</b> Why the fuck would a company that fired you would send you home in a limousine? <br><br><b>3)</b> <b>Why the fuck you dont question Quinn?</b> EVER? IS SOMETHING WRONG WİTH YOUR BRAİN? How did Quinn know you were up in the Canopy room? Or did he? Did he go up there to get you or did he just happen to go up there? And is that why he was suddenly like ‘you need to leave’ when he found out the Canopy room people bought you drinks? He must have known the people up there were shady. And- furthermore- <b>since you suspect that you were slipped something, what is to be done about it? </b><br><br>My reaction would have been immediately asking these questions to myself, then to Quinn to figure out what the fuck was going on. Her reaction? Nothing for a long time but then (after like days!!!) she thinks;<br><blockquote>
  <i>“At some point I would need to ask Quinn if he’d arranged the limo that took me home those weeks ago or if Vincent’s presence tonight was merely a fluke.”</i>
</blockquote><br>YOU THINK?!<br><br>What. The. Hell. The Limusine thing happens in like like 3% in but she is capable of finally thinking about this at 30% of the book (before that, it never even comes to her mind) finally asks him that at 38% but never truly gets the answer because she is too fucking stupid.<br><br><b>4)</b> What the fuck is Quinn's job?<br><br>First she thinks he is a security guard. Then she doesnt. Then she is not sure what it is. Sh never fucking truly wonders about it FOR A LONG TIME. And keeps seeing this guy. <br><br>And it's obvious ok? People call him Mr. Sullivan or Sir. At one point she thinks one of the ground staff was going to salute. Ooo I wonder why? <b>ASK YOURSELF WHYYY!</b><br><br>Also, why would a security guard would do inspection of the site’s media-server facility huh?<br><br>TOO MANY FUCKING CLUES. <br><br><b>5)</b> What’s up with his reaction to the guy in the park? He completely overreacted but do you ask yourself why? NO.<br><br>He puts guards on you but do you ask why? NO.<br><br><b>She says she is too flustered to question him. </b><br><br>THIS GIRL.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431788411ra/14866878.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>She nearly gets raped (because she was drugged) and it doesnt faze her.</b> She doesnt ask any of those questions I mentioned to Quinn. Hell, she doesnt even ask those questions to herself. She never tries to find out the truth. She is never bothered with it. <b>NOTHING FAZES HER.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386473994ra/7373980.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Then here comes other fucking stupid 'coincidences’</b> <br><br>Quinn gets her a new job. Knows her boss. Calls her boss by name. Acts like he's the boss where she works...cause you know HE IS HER FUCKING BOSS. Or his boss's boss. Whatever.<br><br>And it's not a spoiler because from the first page it was too fucking obvious Quinn wasnt a security guard. This girl. This girl doesnt realize the truth until 58% in but even for that somebody had to spell it out for her. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431788411ra/14866879.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I’m not a security guard I am your boss. 5 seconds. It would have taken 5 seconds. But noooo. It doesnt get resolved in until too fucking late.<br><br><b>Other isssues:</b> <br><br><i>1)</i><blockquote>
  <i>“Elizabeth, where she’d continued to insist that Quinn was interested in me and I continued to find the assertion ridiculous; and, therefore, faced with such a man speaking to me in such a way I was wholly unprepared.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br>She consistently thinks he is out of her league. She even insults herself. More than once.<br><br>Most of the book, she is like 'Ohh why would Quinn like me. I’m like so weird.'<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428697643ra/14470774.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>As you can see, Janie is too negative about herself as well as quite clueless.</b><br><br>He tells he is going to a business trip but she thinks he is avoiding him. Then she thinks ‘Why would he continue to text if he was trying to avoid me?’ *rolls eyes* Umm maybe he is not?<br><br> <b>This girl is not capable of a rational thought.</b><br><br><i>2)</i> The reason why she broke up with her ex was ;<br><br>(1-)he cheated on her and <br><br>(2-)he was rich and he was obsessed with taking care of her but she wanted to be financially independent <br><br>The guy she dates next is even more richer, more controlling and loves taking care of her. Soooo..principles can change if the guy is hot I guess right?<br><br><i>3)</i> <b>Quinn was too damn controlling ok?</b> And not in I'm-arrogant-but-in-a-sexy-way way. He came off as a jerk to me. He ordered food/drinks without asking, he bought a house for her without asking, he does this thoughtfull stuff for her but without asking. And the worst part; <b> Janie is too oblivious to see his faults.</b> She is too fucking naive and Quinn definitely is taking advantage of her naivete. <u><br><br> <i> Plus, the misunderstandings between them both were insane and unbelievable, it's as if they were speaking different languages.</i></u> <br><br><i>4)</i><b>This girl cant function without her friends.</b> The only time her brain works is when she gets together with them. One of her friends points out how weird a situation is and only then she realizes the sitiation or how she should really feel. Because <b> most of the book Janie doesnt react, she doesnt think trough, she is just there. She is even more useless than a plant.</b> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Although I tended to obsess about topics like the English vernacular, the height of the average Brazil nut tree, and international date standards, I had a habit of ignoring important details like who drugged me and how did I feel about blacking out only to wake up mostly naked in a strange apartment with seven pieces of furniture.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote>This is my problem with her. She NEVER truly feels the weight of her recklessness and truly understands how dangerous of a situation she'd been in. Not until her friends tells her and even then she still doesnt get it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431788588ra/14866887.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>5)</i>This Quinn guy;<br><br>-Uses his position to get her a job<br><br>-Uses his position to buy her a cellphone<br><br>-Uses his position to spend time with her<br><br>-Uses uses uses..I know Janie is so fucking clueless but it takes like 5 seconds to say ‘NO’ or ask ‘WHY?’. <b>The guy turnes her into a brouhaha of chaos simply by glancing in her direction.</b> It's too fucking embrassing.<br><br><b>OVERALL:</b>I did skip a lot of stuff because the book is filled with awkward sentences and quirky, weird dailogue and quirky and unnecsarily too long paragraphs. <b>I'm fine with awkwardness but oh boy this girl's awkwardness was too damn uncomfortable.</b><br><br>Smart romance my ass.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400521333ra/9684901.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="16406115343878460205" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer993327868" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer10464034567351190565">Finding out what your favorite author likes to read is like getting a sneak peek into their brain. When I saw<b> Amy Harmon</b> sharing her love for this <a href='https://www.facebook.com/authoramyharmon/posts/829523727057852' rel='nofollow noopener'>book</a> I knew I had to read it. <b>I love when authors endorse books.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405112079i/10344083._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Oy vey! Janie is having the <b>"Worst. Day. Ever. It was, no pun intended, an extremely sh*tty day."</b> Her boyfriend cheated on her, she lost her job and now she's stuck in the bathroom with no toilet paper. Our nerdy girl is down on her luck. And to top it off our hero- <b>Sir McHotpants</b> escorts</span>
  <span id="freeText10464034567351190565" style="display:none">Finding out what your favorite author likes to read is like getting a sneak peek into their brain. When I saw<b> Amy Harmon</b> sharing her love for this <a href="https://www.facebook.com/authoramyharmon/posts/829523727057852" rel="nofollow noopener">book</a> I knew I had to read it. <b>I love when authors endorse books.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405112079i/10344083._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oy vey! Janie is having the <b>"Worst. Day. Ever. It was, no pun intended, an extremely sh*tty day."</b> Her boyfriend cheated on her, she lost her job and now she's stuck in the bathroom with no toilet paper. Our nerdy girl is down on her luck. And to top it off our hero- <b>Sir McHotpants</b> escorts her out of the building after being fired. Janie's closest friend and her knitting group are there to console her through this <i>terrible, horrible, no good, very bad day.</i><br><br>Our heroine is nerdy and awkward at best. She has a pension for sprouting off useless facts about random things at the most inappropriate times. <b>"I couldn't help myself as the words tumbled out. It was a sickness."</b> She's a combo of Cher from Clueless, Amy from Big Bang Theory and Betty from Ugly Betty all rolled into one. <br><br>Here's what that combo looks like-&gt;<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405316214i/10381291._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Janie has decided for any future guys she wants them to be <b> 'smart, funny sweet, nice to his family, good looking in an adorkable kind of way.' </b><br> <br>Meet <i>Sir Handsome McHotpants</i> aka Quinn. Quinn is an enigma to Janie. Just when she thinks she has "labeled" him he does something that surprises her and changes her image of him. <br><br>Our quirky heroine and our handsome hero add for a fun enjoyable summer read! <br><br><b>SERIES:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17673307.Neanderthal_Seeks_Human_A_Smart_Romance__Knitting_in_the_City___1_" title="Neanderthal Seeks Human A Smart Romance (Knitting in the City, #1) by Penny Reid" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1364347894s/17673307.jpg" alt="Neanderthal Seeks Human A Smart Romance (Knitting in the City, #1) by Penny Reid" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18001399.Friends_Without_Benefits__Knitting_in_the_City___2_" title="Friends Without Benefits (Knitting in the City, #2) by Penny Reid" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1379202139s/18001399.jpg" alt="Friends Without Benefits (Knitting in the City, #2) by Penny Reid" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20982872.Love_Hacked__Knitting_in_the_City___3_" title="Love Hacked (Knitting in the City, #3) by Penny Reid" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1393966301s/20982872.jpg" alt="Love Hacked (Knitting in the City, #3) by Penny Reid" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20359781.Beauty_and_the_Mustache__Knitting_in_the_City___4_" title="Beauty and the Mustache (Knitting in the City, #4) by Penny Reid" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1388441208s/20359781.jpg" alt="Beauty and the Mustache (Knitting in the City, #4) by Penny Reid" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Can be read as standalones. Each following book is secondary characters from the first book. To find out when more will be released <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/101713-knitting-in-the-city" rel="nofollow noopener">click here.</a><br><br><i>Novella:</i><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18875842.Neanderthal_Marries_Human_A_Smarter_Romance__Knitting_in_the_City___1_5_" title="Neanderthal Marries Human A Smarter Romance (Knitting in the City, #1.5) by Penny Reid" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1385014562s/18875842.jpg" alt="Neanderthal Marries Human A Smarter Romance (Knitting in the City, #1.5) by Penny Reid" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>(#1.5)</span>

<div id="review_1194555685" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1194555685" />
    <a title="S.M. West" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18424676-s-m-west"><img alt="S.M. West" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564323942p2/18424676.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1194555685?book_show_action=true">Feb 08, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="S.M. West" class="user" itemprop="url" name="S.M. West" href="/user/show/18424676-s-m-west">S.M. West</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=favourties">favourties</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=laugh-out-loud">laugh-out-loud</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=uber-sexy-hot-male-lead">uber-sexy-hot-male-lead</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1194555685" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3031918520069281083"><b>5 <i>"You've made me fearless." <br/>"And you've make me a good guy."</i> STARS</b><br/><br/>Yes, I do declare that I love Penny Reid. This is my third book that I've read by Penny and I must say, I am totally captivated and smiling like a dork as I read her books. Even the sad, dangerous or angry moments!<br/><br/>Janie Morris is quirky, dorky, awkward and simply adorable!<br/><br/><b>"Everything about her was unexpected and unique. She was my bright light of eccentricity in a very predictable and ordinary world. She made everything interesti</b></span>
  <span id="freeText3031918520069281083" style="display:none"><b>5 <i>"You've made me fearless." <br>"And you've make me a good guy."</i> STARS</b><br><br>Yes, I do declare that I love Penny Reid. This is my third book that I've read by Penny and I must say, I am totally captivated and smiling like a dork as I read her books. Even the sad, dangerous or angry moments!<br><br>Janie Morris is quirky, dorky, awkward and simply adorable!<br><br><b>"Everything about her was unexpected and unique. She was my bright light of eccentricity in a very predictable and ordinary world. She made everything interesting or funny."</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/xbFjz6R" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451172392i/17513593._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Quinn Sullivan is sexy, controlled, careful and hot!<br><br><b>"My problem is that I miss the obvious; your problem is that you pay too much attention to it."</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/dH05N4n" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451172392i/17513594._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I thoroughly enjoyed this one and her knitting crew were hilarious! Looking forward to more of these gals.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/q3JITwP" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451172392ra/17513595.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I found myself riddled with uncontrollable chuckling as I read the ramblings of Janie! Priceless. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/9Fa1Dn3" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451172392ra/17513596.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>For instance, her thoughts on how she feels about Mr. Quinn McHotPants Sullivan:<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/9fLhSpm" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451172392ra/17513597.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Loved the Epilogue in Quinn's POV. Left me wanting more!! And that's exactly what I'm going to do, diving into <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18875842.Neanderthal_Marries_Human__Knitting_in_the_City___1_5_" title="Neanderthal Marries Human (Knitting in the City, #1.5) by Penny Reid" rel="nofollow noopener">Neanderthal Marries Human</a></span>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/890506453?book_show_action=true">Jul 28, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer890506453" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2551407799303407400"><b>Currently on sale!</b><br/><a href='http://amzn.to/2v5xB33' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon US</a> * <a href='http://amzn.to/2vRSqfQ' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon UK</a><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1501295243ra/23443937.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Neanderthal Seeks Human</i> is a sweet and humorous story about two characters that are complete opposites and very unique in their own way. I honestly don't think I've read a book before where a Hero was as silent as Quinn, but it worked for his character. And even though there wasn't a ton of dialogue with him I still felt like I knew him really well. Without a lot of words and fanfare Quinn let Janie know how much he wanted her ans how much he cared for her.</span>
  <span id="freeText2551407799303407400" style="display:none"><b>Currently on sale!</b><br><a href="http://amzn.to/2v5xB33" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon US</a> * <a href="http://amzn.to/2vRSqfQ" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon UK</a><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1501295243ra/23443937.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Neanderthal Seeks Human</i> is a sweet and humorous story about two characters that are complete opposites and very unique in their own way. I honestly don't think I've read a book before where a Hero was as silent as Quinn, but it worked for his character. And even though there wasn't a ton of dialogue with him I still felt like I knew him really well. Without a lot of words and fanfare Quinn let Janie know how much he wanted her ans how much he cared for her. Though at first Janie was too stuck in her own head to even notice.<br><br>Janie was a quirky and lighthearted heroine, and I really liked reading about her and getting a glimpse at how her mind worked. She was constancy stating trivial facts that I actually found really interesting and I loved that character trait. She also had the tendency to never stop talking but I loved seeing her with Quinn and how he wasn't turned off by her word-vomit. Instead he found her adorable, and it made me happy sigh more than once. <br><br>Janie and Quinn were overall a very cute couple and I have a feeling they may remain my favorite couple from this series even after I read the other books. If you haven't read this book yet, trust me you don't want this just sitting on your TBR.</span>

<div id="review_1156659075" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1156659075" />
    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1156659075?book_show_action=true">Jan 05, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1156659075" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14739502849244772749"><b><i>Neanderthal Seeks Human</i> is a witty romance story about Janie Morris and Quinn <i>McHotpants</i> Sullivan.</b><br/><br/>We first meet Janie on the worst day of her life, it began with her finding out her fiancé cheated on her, breaking her heel on the way to work, getting fired from her job and worst of all: running out of toilet paper in her <i>former</i> companies restroom. If all this happened to me I would be devastated but listening to Janie recount her horrible day had me laughing out loud at how funny she is. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421368093i/13367404._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>On this</span>
  <span id="freeText14739502849244772749" style="display:none"><b><i>Neanderthal Seeks Human</i> is a witty romance story about Janie Morris and Quinn <i>McHotpants</i> Sullivan.</b><br><br>We first meet Janie on the worst day of her life, it began with her finding out her fiancé cheated on her, breaking her heel on the way to work, getting fired from her job and worst of all: running out of toilet paper in her <i>former</i> companies restroom. If all this happened to me I would be devastated but listening to Janie recount her horrible day had me laughing out loud at how funny she is. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421368093i/13367404._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>On this day, the worse day of her life, she is escorted from the building by Sir McHotpants himself - the guy she has been staring at from afar. Janie learns that Sir McHotpants real name is Quinn and is surprised by the level of care and concern he shows to her. After talking with Janie and realizing how incredibly smart she is, Quinn refers Janie for a job at the security company.<br><br>Quinn and Janie begin to build a friendship, it was so fun to see these two people who are both so different communicate. Janie is someone who says exactly whats on her mind and Quinn is the quite brooding type. Janie just ended a long relationship and Quinn doesn’t date, he prefers mutually beneficial relationships. While Janie doesn’t judge that type of relationship, she refuses to be in one herself. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421368093i/13367405._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Watching these two together was addictive.I loved seeing how they worked together and wanted each other to be happy and have peace in the relationship. Both of them were selfless, not one gave more then the other. <br><br><b>
  <i>"God, Quinn, you have no idea how permanent I’d like this to be. I’d like us to be twinkies and cockroaches, death and taxes."</i>
</b><br><br>See Janie isn’t like most people you meet, she is crazy smart and is full of facts. She also has a problem with randomly sharing these facts, so throughout the story Janie would work in a fact. I loved how despite Janie being different then most girls, Quinn was completely enthralled with her. Every time she spoke he was dying to hear what she had to say, it was so endearing. <br><br><b>
  <i>"You know, he is really crazy about you; not crazy like your sister Jem crazy, but trying-to-become-a-better-person crazy.”</i>
</b><br><br>When I finished this one I was just so impressed that Penny Reid even knew all these crazy facts to be able incorporate them in the story, it just made me even more impressed with her. This is my second book I have read by Ms. Reid, since I read <i>The Beauty and the Mustache</i> out of order, and I must say the more I read the more I love. Her writing is so smart, witty, and addictive. Not to mention how good she is at creating diverse characters and I am not saying that lightly. Her characters are completely unique and eccentric, and I have loved all the ones I have met! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421368093i/13367406._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I highly recommend this story. I cannot even begin to describe how much I love Ms. Reid’s writing, if you are looking for something unique, quirky and fun this is the book for you. <br><br><b>
  <i>"…about my worst day ever, which actually turned into one of the best days ever because it was the first time I talked to you and looked you in the eye.”</i>
</b><br><br><i>Sidenote: I did listen to the audio version of this book and narration was great. The narrator was able to execute both parts and read with emotion. </i></span>
  <a data-text-id="14739502849244772749" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1039349719" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1039349719" />
    <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts"><img alt="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378340325p2/17755575.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1039349719?book_show_action=true">Aug 28, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts">Wendy&#39;sThoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Penny Reid Fans, Knitting In the City, Romance</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1039349719" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16738012338989468245"><b>5 Just Great...No...Really, It Is Stars <br/>* * * * * <i>Spoiler Free</i><br/>In the past, when I have been emotionally taken by the writing of an author... I have written blatant love letters to them. If I felt indulgent, I would do that now... I would write and talk about how much I love this story, the author and call it a day. <br/><br/>But, this time I will attempt to talk about the intense feelings and realizations I had while reading this book.<br/><br/>I will set the stage by mentioning this was not my first experience wit</b></span>
  <span id="freeText16738012338989468245" style="display:none"><b>5 Just Great...No...Really, It Is Stars <br>* * * * * <i>Spoiler Free</i><br>In the past, when I have been emotionally taken by the writing of an author... I have written blatant love letters to them. If I felt indulgent, I would do that now... I would write and talk about how much I love this story, the author and call it a day. <br><br>But, this time I will attempt to talk about the intense feelings and realizations I had while reading this book.<br><br>I will set the stage by mentioning this was not my first experience with Penny Reid and The Knitting in the City series. Earlier this year I read blind her book, Loved Hacked. </b> It was part of this series and I was able to enjoy all of it without feeling as if I had missed something from the previous books. If you are curious, this was my review: <i><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/877795138">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a></i><br><br>Penny Reid takes people we know we have met, observed and wondered about... the ones who catch your eye or ear while you are living your life. They are the ones you sometimes randomly think about... they are going about their business... and something intrigues us... we wonder after observing them what will happen after we move on... we saw them do something clever or heard a snippet of a conversation that lent itself to make you think and ponder... <br><br>She creates friendships; meaty, close relationships between women who are so there for each other, it is sometimes overwhelming in the strength of it all. Even the smallest character has thought behind it. Little seeds have been tenderly planted to flourish and grow in later entries. <br><br>But there is a couple of really special accomplishments which struck me... Ms. Reid created in Janie a character many have tried to do; the quirky, pseudo innocent/slightly experienced gal... who is uncomfortable in male-female interactions, etc... <br><br>No, Penny writes of a real woman who has those parts of her personality but had to learn coping mechanisms to survive a childhood that would have destroyed most. She learned her "designated place" in the family and still was able to excel with the brilliance she was endowed.... not using it by lording over others or being overly confident... instead she used it culling information and facts she found compelling... things to think and focus on when her life became too much. This became her escape valve... releasing all her tension but causing some awkward conversations... With those who learned and understood her... it became endearing. <br><br>Janie's mind runs so fast with much being analyzed through a filter of wonder ... it is fascinating... just reading all of the intellectual property slipped in during her conversations would give Jeopardy winners a run for their money. But with all this happening... we never feel talked down to; we never feel it is not part of her... it rings true and we would understand if we were her friend. <br><br>This brings me to the love interest, Quinn...He is not perfect... but he is perfect for Janie. Oh, who am I kidding... he is perfect- but not in an icky over the top way... he is confident yet in his desire for Janie... he must figure her out and work for her. He finds her surprising, strong and challenging in ways he has never experienced..... and he wants to be a better man for her. <br>He has all of the strong "alpha" feelings for her... yet he is smart enough... able to see there are important things she needs in order for them to come together with the way he wants. He is willing to do whatever it will take to make this work and it is a first for him. The chemistry is everything- it is sweet- steamy - hot - dizzy and loving... but not explicit... it doesn't need to be. <br><br>Penny presents some very interesting moral and ethical discussions for us to take away.... she also gives us things which have happened to all of us... and voices all of the same thoughts we had during these times... we see pieces of ourselves in Janie...<br> <br>There is a love story; a mystery of sorts and this introduction to this group of people you would kill to have as friends in your life.<br><br>Well, I tried not to do the "Wendy love letter to the author" review... but when you adore something as much as I did this... I am thinking it is ok to fail...<br><br>The great news is this was the first in the series and the following books have been equally great. Lucky you, you get to read all of them one right after the other... <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17673307.Neanderthal_Seeks_Human__Knitting_in_the_City___1_" title="Neanderthal Seeks Human (Knitting in the City, #1) by Penny Reid" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1364347894l/17673307._SY75_.jpg" alt="Neanderthal Seeks Human (Knitting in the City, #1) by Penny Reid" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>Neanderthal Seeks Human (Knitting in the City, #1) <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1039349719">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a> <br><a <div id="review_669245368" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/669245368" />
    <a title="♡Karlyn P♡" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1131400-karlyn-p"><img alt="♡Karlyn P♡" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1389996373p2/1131400.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/669245368?book_show_action=true">Jul 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♡Karlyn P♡" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♡Karlyn P♡" href="/user/show/1131400-karlyn-p">♡Karlyn P♡</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=read-2014">read-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer669245368" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3863230601637417890"><br/><b>3.5 "What Did I Just Read?!" Stars</b><br/><br/>This book was hilarious... and odd... and funny... and weird... and nutty... and, well I am still wrapping my brain around it.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>Let's start with the players</b>
</blockquote><br/><b>Janine...a.k.a. Neanderthal,...a.k.a. Cuckoo for Cocoa Puffs:</b><br/>Janine is a socially inept, oblivious, gullible, overly analytic moron-slash-genius. Her IQ is off the charts, but her sexual experience level is minimal and she is often clueless to what is really happening around her. She secretly is burning for</span>
  <span id="freeText3863230601637417890" style="display:none"><br /><b>3.5 "What Did I Just Read?!" Stars</b><br /><br />This book was hilarious... and odd... and funny... and weird... and nutty... and, well I am still wrapping my brain around it.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>Let's start with the players</b>
</blockquote><br /><b>Janine...a.k.a. Neanderthal,...a.k.a. Cuckoo for Cocoa Puffs:</b><br />Janine is a socially inept, oblivious, gullible, overly analytic moron-slash-genius. Her IQ is off the charts, but her sexual experience level is minimal and she is often clueless to what is really happening around her. She secretly is burning for the hot security guard nicknamed 'Sir Handsome McHotpants' with the deep blue eyes. <br /><br /><b>Quinn...a.k.a. Human,...a.k.a. Sir Handsome McHotpants:</b><br />Quinn is a man of little words, who tends to speak in one or two sentences TOPS. He is uber rich, beyond handsome, has sparkly teeth, and rescues damsels in distress. He doesn't date, because he is manwhore who simply doesn't need to. Women throw themselves at him. He is clueless about the dating ritual, but finds himself very intrigued with the idea once he sets eyes on the hot quirky red-head accountant Janine. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>Now let's move onto the story</b>
</blockquote><br />We meet Janine when she is having the worst day of her life. She catches her boyfriend cheating on her, loses her job and much more. Quinn comes to her rescue (as he is prone to do over and over!) and helps her find a new job working for his company. Soon, he is her boss -- only Janine is too clueless to figure out this obvious fact. (Yes, her naivety was so cute, but it was also a bit annoying!) <br /><br />Quinn soon believes Janine is in danger of bad guys, and proceeds to try and rescue her a few more times while never letting Janine be the wiser. He also thwarts attempts of her ex-boyfriend Jon (with no 'h') from trying to win her back. Using very little words (because, he only speaks in very short sentences as he is a man of little words) he woos her with kisses and flattery until she agrees to date him. <br /><br />Yadda, yadda, yadda... they smooch a bunch and then fall in love. Oh, and cue 'evil sister' comes for a visit. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>Now my take on this book</b>
</blockquote><br />HOLY SHIT, WHAT DID I JUST READ? Oh, I laughed alright! But I was also confused, to be honest. I wanted to love these two, and at times I really did, but the nutty relationship and her complete cluelessness took its toll on me. The romance both worked and failed for me as I didn't always feel it. I really liked her, but damn... I sometimes wondered if she was an idiot-savant because someone needed to buy this lady a CLUE!<br /><br />While the jokes were hilarious, the romance aspect was a bit weak. The passion and sparks weren't flying off the pages. And the heat level was pretty low, which is a personal disappointment as I like my romances with a good dose of sexy heat. <br /><br />The story was told in first-person through Janine's POV, but we get a nice epilogue from Quinn's POV. The ending really brought this book up a notch for me. It wasn't a winner for me, but I can see why so many enjoyed it. </span>
  <a data-text-id="3863230601637417890" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_581497484" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/581497484" />
    <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy"><img alt="Stacey is Sassy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474185067p2/12062194.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/581497484?book_show_action=true">Apr 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacey is Sassy" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy">Stacey is Sassy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/29412469-neanderthal-seeks-human">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=cont-humour">cont-humour</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=a-re-read">a-re-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=favourites-2013">favourites-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer581497484" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12790131948721009768"><b>Not being perfect is a good thing...</b><br/><br/>This is the kind of story that I can re-read over and over and over again; it just never gets old. The characters are original, quirky and so very interesting, they make me want to stop and think about life and all the weird and wonderful stuff in it. Janie is the kind of character that I would love to meet and spend time with. I'm a bit of an over-thinker, but Janie takes it to another level. I'm envious of her ability to remember all the little titbits that </span>
  <span id="freeText12790131948721009768" style="display:none"><b>Not being perfect is a good thing...</b><br><br>This is the kind of story that I can re-read over and over and over again; it just never gets old. The characters are original, quirky and so very interesting, they make me want to stop and think about life and all the weird and wonderful stuff in it. Janie is the kind of character that I would love to meet and spend time with. I'm a bit of an over-thinker, but Janie takes it to another level. I'm envious of her ability to remember all the little titbits that she shares. I absolutely loved that Quinn appreciated her knowledge and never wanted her to hold back what she's thinking.<br><br>There are so many parts of <i>Neanderthal Seeks Human</i> where I tell myself *remember this, it's a cracker* but of course, by the end, I've forgotten them all. I do remember the feelings of delight and satisfaction, though, so that's just as good. If I could name one section that left me the most satisfied, it would have to be when they're discussing how not being perfect is a good thing. To be honest, I completely agree. I think my hubby is perfect for me but I know he's far from perfect and I'm sure he thinks the same about me. Life would be pretty damn boring if we were all perfect.<br><br>Anyways...if you haven't tried a wee bit of <i>Penny Reid</i> magic yet, I highly recommend starting with this one. You can't go wrong with reading or listening as the narrator does an awesome job.<br><br>I can't help myself, I'm going to listen to <i>Neanderthal Marries Human</i> next.<br><br>**********<br><br><b>First time listening to the audio of <i>Neanderthal Seeks Human</i></b><br><br>Two things -<br><br>1. If you loved reading a story but loved the audio MORE, where do I go from here? 5 stars are the limit. Maybe we need an <b>*To Infinity and Beyond*</b> rating. <i>Neanderthal Seeks Human</i> deserves all the stars.<br><br>2. After reading my old review, I feel extremely guilty that I distracted Penny from her very important work saving the world as a researcher. Did my review push her to split her time between her family, science AND writing? Maybe, all Penny Reid fans should be thanking me. Obviously, my little review made her stop and consider my needs. Yes, I am extremely grateful that she takes the time out of her busy schedule to write. Maybe, Penny, you could do me a favour and drop me a quick line to absolve me from my guilt. It's weighing heavily on my conscience, after all. (Wink, wink...oh, the naivety of a book reviewer in 2013).<br><br>I LOVED THE AUDIO!! It was such a fun experience seeing everyone back in the beginning. It was almost like I could see Penny's notes for future books. Little sayings and character quirks that we now know more about. Everybody seems so sweet and innocent, hiding their strong personalities. I loved knowing where they were heading.<br><br>I'm keeping on with the audios for the series and I can't wait to see Nicoletta again. <br><br>****Old Review****<br><br>I started reading this book from a recommendation on Kristen Ashley addicts group. The first 10% of this book I was a little unsure if it was my style or not. Considering this is Ms Reid's first full-length novel, it was written really well. My only complaint is that there was too much internal dialogue at first. The paragraphs were really long and I started to lose interest. My husband walked in while I was reading this book and I said to him I would give it till 15% to decide.<br><br>I'm glad I did. Once I got past the too long internal dialogue at the beginning and the characters were all introduced, I really like it.<br><br>Ms Reid I know you said you like your current job and all...but maybe you could work part-time and write some more. I would definitely read more of your books and would like to hear about more of the characters in the knitting group.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1548709401i/26982519.jpg" width="300" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="12790131948721009768" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText7815993218826866724" style="display:none">4.5 LOVE Quinn Sir Handsome McHotpants STARS!!!!<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/imagejpg1_zpsfeb22641.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397085364i/9229011._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo imagejpg1_zpsfeb22641.jpg" width="370" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I love my ROMCOM stories and <b>"Neanderthal Seeks Human"</b> had me laughing and swooning in equal measure.<br>Janie Morris is having a day from hell.<br>She just broke up with her boyfriend, after having found out he cheated on her.<br>The heel of her show broke off on a sewer grate.<br>Spilled coffee on her favorite blouse and she's just lost her job due to downsizing.<br>To top the day she is having, she's being escorted out of the office by the HOT security guard she had been ogling for the past month, Sir Handsome McHotpants!!<br><br><br>Seems like a bad day right?<br>Actually, her luck really starts to change from here in the BEST of ways.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/imagejpg2_zps97f29cd1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397085364i/9229012._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo imagejpg2_zps97f29cd1.jpg" width="375" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>McHotpants aka Quinn Sullivan, sets her up with a job interview.<br>It's obvious that Quinn is very much attracted to Janie, but Janie is utterly clueless.<br>She sees herself as this big headed Neanderthal and Quinn is one of the beautiful people who would never give her a second glance.<br>I loved how completely goofy she would get whenever she was alone with him.<br>Her ramblings were very cute and endearing.<br>Quinn seemed to enjoy all the little tidbits of scientific and mathematical information that Janie would ramble on to him about when she was feeling awkward around him.<br><br><br><b>I was in awkwardly shaped head Neanderthal league, and he was in the hot ninja millionaire league.</b><br><br><br><br>Janie gets the job at the company that Quinn set up the interview for her and come to find out later on that Quinn is the owner of said company, which will have her questioning why she got the job and will she be able to keep it if their relationship progresses or ends.<br><br><br><br>There are a great group of friends that Janie meets on a weekly basis to Knit with and they will be there for her when she needs them the most.<br>I loved how they were always cheering her on and how protective they were of her if they felt someone was trying to hurt her.<br><br><br><br>This story even has a bit of action and Quinn is just full of surprises.<br>The romance was slow to build but oh so sweet and the sexy time was very PG but it never hindered my love for the story and I still ended up swooning pretty hard over Quinn.<br><br><br><b>For the love of Thor, I was missing him even when we were in the same room together. The force of the feelings and the virtually all-consuming nature of them made me want to hide under my desk until my brain and my heart and my vagina came to a consensus.</b><br><br><br><br><b>I lost myself to him and to myself; to trust and to faith; and in that moment, I was fearless.</b><br><br><br><br>I'm looking forward to the remaining books in the series and have definitely added Penny to my favorite authors list. :)<br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_1226987059" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1226987059" />
    <a title="Ingie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15589375-ingie"><img alt="Ingie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1477339772p2/15589375.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1226987059?book_show_action=true">Mar 14, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ingie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ingie" href="/user/show/15589375-ingie">Ingie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook " href="/book/show/23357564-neanderthal-seeks-human">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=books-i-read-2015">books-i-read-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=romance-m-f-audio">romance-m-f-audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=romance-m-f-contemporary">romance-m-f-contemporary</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1226987059" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer139847678123825382"><i>Written April 10, 2015</i><br/><br/><b>3.8 Stars - Hilarious funny and sweet "romcom" with a wacky heroine I never will forget</b><br/><br/>This was a Kindle freebie some time ago and it was possible to add a low-priced <i>"whispersynk for voice"</i> audiobook (just $2.30). After reading a lot of happy reviews was the 14:20 hrs audiobook narrated by <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/3133768.Jennifer_Grace' title='Jennifer Grace' rel='nofollow noopener'>Jennifer Grace</a> mine too. <br/><blockquote>
<a href='http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/90452c2d-c479-4aae-a1de-29707fdbe0d6_zpsy76bwuxh.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424367709i/13752681.jpg' alt=' photo 90452c2d-c479-4aae-a1de-29707fdbe0d6_zpsy76bwuxh.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/>‘I decided, as I succumbed to sleep, that men should come with manuals, subtitles, and reset buttons.’</blockquote><br/><b>A quick satisfied tap-dance...</b><br/>Besides the large number of </span>
  <span id="freeText139847678123825382" style="display:none"><i>Written April 10, 2015</i><br><br><b>3.8 Stars - Hilarious funny and sweet "romcom" with a wacky heroine I never will forget</b><br><br>This was a Kindle freebie some time ago and it was possible to add a low-priced <i>"whispersynk for voice"</i> audiobook (just $2.30). After reading a lot of happy reviews was the 14:20 hrs audiobook narrated by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/3133768.Jennifer_Grace" title="Jennifer Grace" rel="nofollow noopener">Jennifer Grace</a> mine too. <br><blockquote>
<a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/90452c2d-c479-4aae-a1de-29707fdbe0d6_zpsy76bwuxh.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424367709i/13752681.jpg" alt=" photo 90452c2d-c479-4aae-a1de-29707fdbe0d6_zpsy76bwuxh.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>‘I decided, as I succumbed to sleep, that men should come with manuals, subtitles, and reset buttons.’</blockquote><br><b>A quick satisfied tap-dance...</b><br>Besides the large number of hours a wonderful entertaining listening. Not only fun, outrageously fun time to time. <br><br>***********************************************<br><br><i>Neanderthal Seeks Human</i> is a hilarious funny romantic novel (more Chick-Lit than steamy Romance tough) about the super "geeky nerd" girl <b>Janie Morris</b> and <b>Quinn Sullivan</b> (aka <i>Sir McHotpants</i>). <br><br>The same day Janie is losing her boyfriend, apartment, and job starts the very gorgeous handsome <i>Sir McHotpants</i> to appear in her messy life. <br><blockquote>
<a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/90452c2d-c479-4aae-a1de-29707fdbe0d6_zpsy76bwuxh.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424367709i/13752681.jpg" alt=" photo 90452c2d-c479-4aae-a1de-29707fdbe0d6_zpsy76bwuxh.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>‘If we were in Victorian England I would have called him dashing; but, since we lived in the 21st century I would have to settle for the wordier GQ model hot.’<br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Couple%20in%20love/image.jpg8_zpsx0qkxpr2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428600900i/14450779.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg8_zpsx0qkxpr2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>“What are you doing tonight?” <br>“I’m meeting my knitting group at seven o’clock.” <br>“I didn’t know you knit.” He lifted his eyebrows. <br>“I don’t.” <br>His eyebrows lifted slightly higher . “Oh, ok. Well, how about later?”<br>I answered truthfully. “I was planning to sort my comic books based on level of second-wave feminist influence.”</blockquote><br>***********************************************<br><br><b>I like just about everything about this story</b>, with one exception: This book is to be honest a bit too long. I must admit that my interest wavered towards the end. Fourteen hours without more suspense action, only misty (hidden) sexy heat and no real speed of events made this book a bit slow for me. Besides that, I have only praise. <br><br><b>This heroine Janie is among the funniest, most clever, brightest and craziest</b> I've met in a long time. It was a pleasure to follow all those winding sidetrack her (incredible brain) thoughts and ideas are taking. ~ I laughed so that tears broke out a few times.<br><blockquote>“Because I’m not thinking about the fiber content in stain- resistant carpet.” My eyes remained stubbornly shut. <br>“What does that mean?” <br>“It means…” I lifted my lids and found him surveying me with simple curiosity. I swallowed a new thickness in my throat, knowing that I needed to tell him the truth. “It means my brain finds you more interesting than all the really interesting trivial facts I could be contemplating or researching at present.” <br>His answering smile was leisurely and measured. “I think that’s the nicest thing anyone has ever said to me.”<br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/90452c2d-c479-4aae-a1de-29707fdbe0d6_zpsy76bwuxh.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1424367709i/13752681.jpg" alt=" photo 90452c2d-c479-4aae-a1de-29707fdbe0d6_zpsy76bwuxh.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</blockquote><br>The hero Quinn is sexy, mysterious and a real man's man. He is just wonderful and perfect in the role of astonished and amused admirer. It would have been fun with some chapters from his point of view as well. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ As it was now was he unfortunately often not more than an 'acquaintance' for me. I had wanted to get to know him much better to be able to fall in love just as Janie did. ~ ...Then we got the epilogue. Yay!!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>***********************************************<br><br><b>The audiobook edition?</b><br>This new narrator for me, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/3133768.Jennifer_Grace" title="Jennifer Grace" rel="nofollow noopener">Jennifer Grace</a> was very pleasant to listening to. I enjoyed her way of telling me this story. <br><br>***********************************************<br><br><b>A Good One!! </b><br>It's been a while since I usually prefered books in this <i>chick-lit / romcom</i> genre (ten or fiften years ago there were many new ones in my bookcase). I'm glad I took the chance this week. <i>Neanderthal Seeks Human</i> is not so explicit in the romance heat as many romances I read nowadays, but in my opinion is that outweighed by everything else good that are offered here. <br><br>This author is really well worth a second try later. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5997227.Penny_Reid" title="Penny Reid" rel="nofollow noopener">Penny Reid</a> shows here a big talent for very funny scenes and subtle delightful characters.<br><br><b>I LIKE - crazy geek heroines</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="139847678123825382" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

<span id="freeTextContainer7206663396432745146">Reread and it was so much fun as I know how the relationship of Quinn and Janie evolves in next six books. They are weird and misfit but they gel perfectly together. </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1916844292?book_show_action=true">Feb 17, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hannah G" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hannah G" href="/user/show/58220052-hannah-g">Hannah G</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1916844292" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18285244923835353108">Overall I'm rating this book 3.75 stars. This was my first book by the author and I ended up enjoying this. Janie was hard for me, as the book went on I liked her less and less. She was very judgemental and liked to label people. What I did like about her was her random factoids and overall her charater was well developed. Quinn was the perfect man for this book. I liked his character and he made this read 100s of times better. The romance in this book was lacking a tad. I felt that the relation</span>
  <span id="freeText18285244923835353108" style="display:none">Overall I'm rating this book 3.75 stars. This was my first book by the author and I ended up enjoying this. Janie was hard for me, as the book went on I liked her less and less. She was very judgemental and liked to label people. What I did like about her was her random factoids and overall her charater was well developed. Quinn was the perfect man for this book. I liked his character and he made this read 100s of times better. The romance in this book was lacking a tad. I felt that the relationship progression went to quickly. It would have been better to see the characters connect and not Janies problems. This wasn't boring and it definitely entertained me. I did enjoy reading this and it was sweet. I'll definitely continue this book series. <br /><br />Side note: The title of this book has nothing to do with the storyline. I award this book with Bad Title Syndrome.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18285244923835353108" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked

    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {

    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

The really, really hot Irish rugby player who plays the position of ‘hooker’ in the RLI (Rugby League International)?
